\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00319}00319     \textcolor{comment}{// Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00320}00320     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() = push window to the stack and start appending to it. End() = pop window from the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00321}00321     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Passing 'bool* p\_open != NULL' shows a window-\/closing widget in the upper-\/right corner of the window,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00322}00322     \textcolor{comment}{//   which clicking will set the boolean to false when clicked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00323}00323     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may append multiple times to the same window during the same frame by calling Begin()/End() pairs multiple times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00324}00324     \textcolor{comment}{//   Some information such as 'flags' or 'p\_open' will only be considered by the first call to Begin().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00325}00325     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() return false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00326}00326     \textcolor{comment}{//   anything to the window. Always call a matching End() for each Begin() call, regardless of its return value!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00327}00327     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00328}00328     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00329}00329     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00330}00330     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note that the bottom of window stack always contains a window called "{}Debug"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00331}00331     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          Begin(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* name, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00334}00334     \textcolor{comment}{// Child Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00335}00335     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use child windows to begin into a self-\/contained independent scrolling/clipping regions within a host window. Child windows can embed their own child.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00336}00336     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For each independent axis of 'size': ==0.0f: use remaining host window size / >0.0f: fixed size / <0.0f: use remaining window size minus abs(size) / Each axis can use a different mode, e.g. ImVec2(0,400).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00337}00337     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ BeginChild() returns false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting anything to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00338}00338     \textcolor{comment}{//   Always call a matching EndChild() for each BeginChild() call, regardless of its return value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00339}00339     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00340}00340     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00341}00341     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00463}00463     \textcolor{comment}{// ID stack/scopes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00464}00464     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the FAQ (docs/FAQ.md or http://dearimgui.org/faq) for more details about how ID are handled in dear imgui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00465}00465     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those questions are answered and impacted by understanding of the ID stack system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00466}00466     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: Why is my widget not reacting when I click on it?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00467}00467     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have widgets with an empty label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00468}00468     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have multiple widgets with the same label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00469}00469     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Short version: ID are hashes of the entire ID stack. If you are creating widgets in a loop you most likely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00470}00470     \textcolor{comment}{//   want to push a unique identifier (e.g. object pointer, loop index) to uniquely differentiate them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00471}00471     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also use the "{}Label\#\#foobar"{} syntax within widget label to distinguish them from each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00472}00472     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In this header file we use the "{}label"{}/"{}name"{} terminology to denote a string that will be displayed + used as an ID,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00473}00473     \textcolor{comment}{//   whereas "{}str\_id"{} denote a string that is only used as an ID and not normally displayed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00474}00474     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00475}00475     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_begin, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_end);       \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00476}00476     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* ptr\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push pointer into the ID stack (will hash pointer).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00477}00477     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} int\_id);                                             \textcolor{comment}{// push integer into the ID stack (will hash integer).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00478}00478     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PopID();                                                        \textcolor{comment}{// pop from the ID stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00479}00479     IMGUI\_API ImGuiID       GetID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                      \textcolor{comment}{// calculate unique ID (hash of whole ID stack + given parameter). e.g. if you want to query into ImGuiStorage yourself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00480}00480     IMGUI\_API ImGuiID       GetID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_begin, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_end);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00483}00483     \textcolor{comment}{// Widgets: Text}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00484}00484     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TextUnformatted(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* text, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* text\_end = NULL); \textcolor{comment}{// raw text without formatting. Roughly equivalent to Text("{}\%s"{}, text) but: A) doesn't require null terminated string if 'text\_end' is specified, B) it's faster, no memory copy is done, no buffer size limits, recommended for long chunks of text.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00524}00524     \textcolor{comment}{// Widgets: Drag Sliders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00525}00525     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ CTRL+Click on any drag box to turn them into an input box. Manually input values aren't clamped by default and can go off-\/bounds. Use ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp to always clamp.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00526}00526     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For all the Float2/Float3/Float4/Int2/Int3/Int4 versions of every functions, note that a 'float v[X]' function argument is the same as 'float* v',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00527}00527     \textcolor{comment}{//   the array syntax is just a way to document the number of elements that are expected to be accessible. You can pass address of your first element out of a contiguous set, e.g. \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00528}00528     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Adjust format string to decorate the value with a prefix, a suffix, or adapt the editing and display precision e.g. "{}\%.3f"{} -\/> 1.234; "{}\%5.2f secs"{} -\/> 01.23 secs; "{}Biscuit: \%.0f"{} -\/> Biscuit: 1; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00529}00529     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Format string may also be set to NULL or use the default format ("{}\%f"{} or "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00530}00530     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Speed are per-\/pixel of mouse movement (v\_speed=0.2f: mouse needs to move by 5 pixels to increase value by 1). For gamepad/keyboard navigation, minimum speed is Max(v\_speed, minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00531}00531     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_min < v\_max to clamp edits to given limits. Note that CTRL+Click manual input can override those limits if ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00532}00532     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_max = FLT\_MAX / INT\_MAX etc to avoid clamping to a maximum, same with v\_min = -\/FLT\_MAX / INT\_MIN to avoid clamping to a minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00533}00533     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use the same sets of flags for DragXXX() and SliderXXX() functions as the features are the same and it makes it easier to swap them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00534}00534     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Legacy: Pre-\/1.78 there are DragXXX() function signatures that takes a final `float power=1.0f' argument instead of the `ImGuiSliderFlags flags=0' argument.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00535}00535     \textcolor{comment}{//   If you get a warning converting a float to ImGuiSliderFlags, read https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/3361}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00670}00670     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups, Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00671}00671     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They block normal mouse hovering detection (and therefore most mouse interactions) behind them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00672}00672     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00673}00673     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Their visibility state (\string~bool) is held internally instead of being held by the programmer as we are used to with regular Begin*() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00674}00674     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The 3 properties above are related: we need to retain popup visibility state in the library because popups may be closed as any time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00675}00675     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can bypass the hovering restriction by using ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup when calling IsItemHovered() or IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00676}00676     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Popup identifiers are relative to the current ID stack, so OpenPopup and BeginPopup generally needs to be at the same level of the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00677}00677     \textcolor{comment}{//    This is sometimes leading to confusing mistakes. May rework this in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00678}00678 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00712}00712 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00713}00713     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00714}00714     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Full-\/featured replacement for old Columns API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00715}00715     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See Demo-\/>Tables for demo code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00716}00716     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See top of imgui\_tables.cpp for general commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00717}00717     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See ImGuiTableFlags\_ and ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_ enums for a description of available flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00718}00718     \textcolor{comment}{// The typical call flow is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00719}00719     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 1. Call BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00720}00720     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 2. Optionally call TableSetupColumn() to submit column name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00721}00721     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 3. Optionally call TableSetupScrollFreeze() to request scroll freezing of columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00722}00722     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 4. Optionally call TableHeadersRow() to submit a header row. Names are pulled from TableSetupColumn() data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00723}00723     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Populate contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00724}00724     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ In most situations you can use TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex(N) to start appending into a column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00725}00725     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ If you are using tables as a sort of grid, where every columns is holding the same type of contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00726}00726     \textcolor{comment}{//      you may prefer using TableNextColumn() instead of TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00727}00727     \textcolor{comment}{//      TableNextColumn() will automatically wrap-\/around into the next row if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00728}00728     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ IMPORTANT: Comparatively to the old Columns() API, we need to call TableNextColumn() for the first column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00729}00729     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Summary of possible call flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00730}00730     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00731}00731     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(0) -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(1) -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00732}00732     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00733}00733     \textcolor{comment}{//                          TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK: TableNextColumn() automatically gets to next row!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00734}00734     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow()                           -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{})                                               // Not OK! Missing TableSetColumnIndex() or TableNextColumn()! Text will not appear!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00735}00735     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00736}00736     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Call EndTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00737}00737     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginTable(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column, ImGuiTableFlags flags = 0, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& outer\_size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0.0f, 0.0f), \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inner\_width = 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00738}00738     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndTable();                                 \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndTable() if BeginTable() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00739}00739     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableNextRow(ImGuiTableRowFlags row\_flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min\_row\_height = 0.0f); \textcolor{comment}{// append into the first cell of a new row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00740}00740     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableNextColumn();                          \textcolor{comment}{// append into the next column (or first column of next row if currently in last column). Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00741}00741     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableSetColumnIndex(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n);          \textcolor{comment}{// append into the specified column. Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00742}00742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00743}00743     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Headers \& Columns declaration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00744}00744     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupColumn() to specify label, resizing policy, default width/weight, id, various other flags etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00745}00745     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableHeadersRow() to create a header row and automatically submit a TableHeader() for each column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00746}00746     \textcolor{comment}{//   Headers are required to perform: reordering, sorting, and opening the context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00747}00747     \textcolor{comment}{//   The context menu can also be made available in columns body using ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00748}00748     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may manually submit headers using TableNextRow() + TableHeader() calls, but this is only useful in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00749}00749     \textcolor{comment}{//   some advanced use cases (e.g. adding custom widgets in header row).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00750}00750     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupScrollFreeze() to lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00751}00751     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableSetupColumn(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, ImGuiTableColumnFlags flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} init\_width\_or\_weight = 0.0f, ImGuiID user\_id = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00795}00795     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA API] Enable with io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_DockingEnable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00796}00796     \textcolor{comment}{// Note: You can use most Docking facilities without calling any API. You DO NOT need to call DockSpace() to use Docking!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00797}00797     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Drag from window title bar or their tab to dock/undock. Hold SHIFT to disable docking/undocking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00798}00798     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Drag from window menu button (upper-\/left button) to undock an entire node (all windows).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00799}00799     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When io.ConfigDockingWithShift == true, you instead need to hold SHIFT to \_enable\_ docking/undocking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00800}00800     \textcolor{comment}{// About dockspaces:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00801}00801     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use DockSpace() to create an explicit dock node \_within\_ an existing window. See Docking demo for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00802}00802     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use DockSpaceOverViewport() to create an explicit dock node covering the screen or a specific viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00803}00803     \textcolor{comment}{//   This is often used with ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_PassthruCentralNode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00804}00804     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: Dockspaces need to be submitted \_before\_ any window they can host. Submit it early in your frame!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00805}00805     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: Dockspaces need to be kept alive if hidden, otherwise windows docked into it will be undocked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00806}00806     \textcolor{comment}{//   e.g. if you have multiple tabs with a dockspace inside each tab: submit the non-\/visible dockspaces with ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_KeepAliveOnly.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01078}01078 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01079}01079 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(), IsPopupOpen() functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01080}01080 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To be backward compatible with older API which took an 'int mouse\_button = 1' argument, we need to treat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01081}01081 \textcolor{comment}{//   small flags values as a mouse button index, so we encode the mouse button in the first few bits of the flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01082}01082 \textcolor{comment}{//   It is therefore guaranteed to be legal to pass a mouse button index in ImGuiPopupFlags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01083}01083 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For the same reason, we exceptionally default the ImGuiPopupFlags argument of BeginPopupContextXXX functions to 1 instead of 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01084}01084 \textcolor{comment}{//   IMPORTANT: because the default parameter is 1 (==ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight), if you rely on the default parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01085}01085 \textcolor{comment}{//   and want to another another flag, you need to pass in the ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01086}01086 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Multiple buttons currently cannot be combined/or-\/ed in those functions (we could allow it later).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01087}01087 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiPopupFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01088}01088 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01089}01089     ImGuiPopupFlags\_None                    = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01090}01090     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonLeft         = 0,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Left Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 0 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Left)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01091}01091     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight        = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Right Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 1 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Right)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01092}01092     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMiddle       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Middle Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 2 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Middle)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01093}01093     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMask\_        = 0x1F,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01094}01094     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonDefault\_     = 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01095}01095     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// For OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(): don't open if there's already a popup at the same level of the popup stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01096}01096     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverItems         = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContextWindow(): don't return true when hovering items, only when hovering empty space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01097}01097     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): ignore the ImGuiID parameter and test for any popup.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01098}01098     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel           = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): search/test at any level of the popup stack (default test in the current level)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01099}01099     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopup                = ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId | ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01100}01100 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01101}01101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01102}01102 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::Selectable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01103}01103 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiSelectableFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01104}01104 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01156}01156 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01157}01157 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01158}01158 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important! Sizing policies have complex and subtle side effects, much more so than you would expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01159}01159 \textcolor{comment}{//   Read comments/demos carefully + experiment with live demos to get acquainted with them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01160}01160 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DEFAULT sizing policies are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01161}01161 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit    if ScrollX is on, or if host window has ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01162}01162 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame if ScrollX is off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01163}01163 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01164}01164 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch with same weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01165}01165 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Stretch (default), Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01166}01166 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns (if any) will generally obtain their requested width (unless the table cannot fit them all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01167}01167 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Stretch Columns will share the remaining width according to their respective weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01168}01168 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Mixed Fixed/Stretch columns is possible but has various side-\/effects on resizing behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01169}01169 \textcolor{comment}{//      The typical use of mixing sizing policies is: any number of LEADING Fixed columns, followed by one or two TRAILING Stretch columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01170}01170 \textcolor{comment}{//      (this is because the visible order of columns have subtle but necessary effects on how they react to manual resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01171}01171 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01172}01172 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01173}01173 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Fixed/Auto mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01174}01174 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns can be enlarged as needed. Table will show an horizontal scrollbar if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01175}01175 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ When using auto-\/resizing (non-\/resizable) fixed columns, querying the content width to use item right-\/alignment e.g. SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN) doesn't make sense, would create a feedback loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01176}01176 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Using Stretch columns OFTEN DOES NOT MAKE SENSE if ScrollX is on, UNLESS you have specified a value for 'inner\_width' in BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01177}01177 \textcolor{comment}{//      If you specify a value for 'inner\_width' then effectively the scrolling space is known and Stretch or mixed Fixed/Stretch columns become meaningful again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01178}01178 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read on documentation at the top of imgui\_tables.cpp for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01179}01179 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01180}01180 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01181}01181     \textcolor{comment}{// Features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01182}01182     ImGuiTableFlags\_None                       = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01183}01183     ImGuiTableFlags\_Resizable                  = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable resizing columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01184}01184     ImGuiTableFlags\_Reorderable                = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable reordering columns in header row (need calling TableSetupColumn() + TableHeadersRow() to display headers)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01185}01185     ImGuiTableFlags\_Hideable                   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable hiding/disabling columns in context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01186}01186     ImGuiTableFlags\_Sortable                   = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable sorting. Call TableGetSortSpecs() to obtain sort specs. Also see ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti and ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01187}01187     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoSavedSettings            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable persisting columns order, width and sort settings in the .ini file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01188}01188     ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody          = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Right-\/click on columns body/contents will display table context menu. By default it is available in TableHeadersRow().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01189}01189     \textcolor{comment}{// Decorations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01190}01190     ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg                      = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Set each RowBg color with ImGuiCol\_TableRowBg or ImGuiCol\_TableRowBgAlt (equivalent of calling TableSetBgColor with ImGuiTableBgFlags\_RowBg0 on each row manually)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01191}01191     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders between rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01192}01192     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH              = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders at the top and bottom.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01193}01193     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV              = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders between columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01194}01194     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV              = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders on the left and right sides.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01195}01195     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersH                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01196}01196     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersV                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01197}01197     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw inner borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01198}01198     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw outer borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01199}01199     ImGuiTableFlags\_Borders                    = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw all borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01200}01200     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBody            = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01201}01201     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBodyUntilResize = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body until hovered for resize (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01202}01202     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Policy (read above for defaults)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01203}01203     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit             = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching contents width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01204}01204     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame            = 2 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching the maximum contents width of all columns. Implicitly enable ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01205}01205     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp          = 3 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights proportional to each columns contents widths.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01206}01206     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame          = 4 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights all equal, unless overridden by TableSetupColumn().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01207}01207     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Extra Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01208}01208     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendX              = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer width auto-\/fit to columns, overriding outer\_size.x value. Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled and Stretch columns are not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01209}01209     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY              = 1 << 17,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer height stop exactly at outer\_size.y (prevent auto-\/extending table past the limit). Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled. Data below the limit will be clipped and not visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01210}01210     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible       = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable keeping column always minimally visible when ScrollX is off and table gets too small. Not recommended if columns are resizable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01211}01211     ImGuiTableFlags\_PreciseWidths              = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable distributing remainder width to stretched columns (width allocation on a 100-\/wide table with 3 columns: Without this flag: 33,33,34. With this flag: 33,33,33). With larger number of columns, resizing will appear to be less smooth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01212}01212     \textcolor{comment}{// Clipping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01213}01213     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoClip                     = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable clipping rectangle for every individual columns (reduce draw command count, items will be able to overflow into other columns). Generally incompatible with TableSetupScrollFreeze().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01214}01214     \textcolor{comment}{// Padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01215}01215     ImGuiTableFlags\_PadOuterX                  = 1 << 21,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is on. Enable outer-\/most padding. Generally desirable if you have headers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01216}01216     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadOuterX                = 1 << 22,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is off. Disable outer-\/most padding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01217}01217     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadInnerX                = 1 << 23,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable inner padding between columns (double inner padding if BordersOuterV is on, single inner padding if BordersOuterV is off).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01218}01218     \textcolor{comment}{// Scrolling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01219}01219     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollX                    = 1 << 24,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable horizontal scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size. Changes default sizing policy. Because this create a child window, ScrollY is currently generally recommended when using ScrollX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01220}01220     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollY                    = 1 << 25,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable vertical scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01221}01221     \textcolor{comment}{// Sorting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01222}01222     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti                  = 1 << 26,  \textcolor{comment}{// Hold shift when clicking headers to sort on multiple column. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount > 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01223}01223     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate               = 1 << 27,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow no sorting, disable default sorting. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount == 0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01224}01224 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01225}01225     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Combinations and masks}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01227}01227 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01235}01235 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::TableSetupColumn()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01236}01236 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01237}01237 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01238}01238     \textcolor{comment}{// Input configuration flags}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01239}01239     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_None                  = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01240}01240     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_Disabled              = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Overriding/master disable flag: hide column, won't show in context menu (unlike calling TableSetColumnEnabled() which manipulates the user accessible state)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01241}01241     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_DefaultHide           = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Default as a hidden/disabled column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01242}01242     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_DefaultSort           = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Default as a sorting column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01243}01243     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch          = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Column will stretch. Preferable with horizontal scrolling disabled (default if table sizing policy is \_SizingStretchSame or \_SizingStretchProp).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01244}01244     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Column will not stretch. Preferable with horizontal scrolling enabled (default if table sizing policy is \_SizingFixedFit and table is resizable).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01245}01245     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_NoResize              = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable manual resizing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01246}01246     ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_NoReorder             = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable manual reordering this column, this will also prevent other columns from crossing over this column.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01284}01284 \textcolor{comment}{// Enum for ImGui::TableSetBgColor()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01285}01285 \textcolor{comment}{// Background colors are rendering in 3 layers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01286}01286 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 0: draw with RowBg0 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg0 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01287}01287 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 1: draw with RowBg1 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg1 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01288}01288 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 2: draw with CellBg color if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01289}01289 \textcolor{comment}{// The purpose of the two row/columns layers is to let you decide if a background color changes should override or blend with the existing color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01290}01290 \textcolor{comment}{// When using ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg on the table, each row has the RowBg0 color automatically set for odd/even rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01291}01291 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg0 target, your color will override the existing RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01292}01292 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg1 or ColumnBg1 target, your color will blend over the RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01293}01293 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableBgTarget\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01294}01294 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01295}01295     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_None                         = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01296}01296     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg0                       = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 0 (generally used for background, automatically set when ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg is used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01297}01297     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg1                       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 1 (generally used for selection marking)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01298}01298     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_CellBg                       = 3         \textcolor{comment}{// Set cell background color (top-\/most color)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01299}01299 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01584}01584     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableSetMousePos   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct navigation to move the mouse cursor. May be useful on TV/console systems where moving a virtual mouse is awkward. Will update io.MousePos and set io.WantSetMousePos=true. If enabled you MUST honor io.WantSetMousePos requests in your backend, otherwise ImGui will react as if the mouse is jumping around back and forth.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01593}01593     \textcolor{comment}{// When using viewports it is recommended that your default value for ImGuiCol\_WindowBg is opaque (Alpha=1.0) so transition to a viewport won't be noticeable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01594}01594     ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable        = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Viewport enable flags (require both ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports + ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasViewports set by the respective backends)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01595}01595     ImGuiConfigFlags\_DpiEnableScaleViewports= 1 << 14,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA: Don't use] FIXME-\/DPI: Reposition and resize imgui windows when the DpiScale of a viewport changed (mostly useful for the main viewport hosting other window). Note that resizing the main window itself is up to your application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01596}01596     ImGuiConfigFlags\_DpiEnableScaleFonts    = 1 << 15,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA: Don't use] FIXME-\/DPI: Request bitmap-\/scaled fonts to match DpiScale. This is a very low-\/quality workaround. The correct way to handle DPI is \_currently\_ to replace the atlas and/or fonts in the Platform\_OnChangedViewport callback, but this is all early work in progress.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01609}01609     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasSetMousePos        = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports io.WantSetMousePos requests to reposition the OS mouse position (only used if ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableSetMousePos is set).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01610}01610     ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasVtxOffset  = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Renderer supports ImDrawCmd::VtxOffset. This enables output of large meshes (64K+ vertices) while still using 16-\/bit indices.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01614}01614     ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasMouseHoveredViewport=1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Platform supports setting io.MouseHoveredViewport to the viewport directly under the mouse \_IGNORING\_ viewports with the ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs flag and \_REGARDLESS\_ of whether another viewport is focused and may be capturing the mouse. This information is \_NOT EASY\_ to provide correctly with most high-\/level engines! Don't set this without studying \_carefully\_ how the backends handle ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01615}01615     ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasViewports  = 1 << 12   \textcolor{comment}{// Backend Renderer supports multiple viewports.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01836}01836 \textcolor{comment}{// We call C++ constructor on own allocated memory via the placement "{}new(ptr) Type()"{} syntax.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01851}01851 \textcolor{comment}{// Lightweight std::vector<>-\/like class to avoid dragging dependencies (also, some implementations of STL with debug enabled are absurdly slow, we bypass it so our code runs fast in debug).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01852}01852 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01853}01853 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You generally do NOT need to care or use this ever. But we need to make it available in imgui.h because some of our public structures are relying on it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01854}01854 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use std-\/like naming convention here, which is a little unusual for this codebase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01855}01855 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: clear() frees memory, resize(0) keep the allocated buffer. We use resize(0) a lot to intentionally recycle allocated buffers across frames and amortize our costs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01856}01856 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: our implementation does NOT call C++ constructors/destructors, we treat everything as raw data! This is intentional but be extra mindful of that,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01857}01857 \textcolor{comment}{//   Do NOT use this class as a std::vector replacement in your own code! Many of the structures used by dear imgui can be safely initialized by a zero-\/memset.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01858}01858 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02350}02350 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Key-\/>Value storage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02351}02351 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically you don't have to worry about this since a storage is held within each Window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02352}02352 \textcolor{comment}{// We use it to e.g. store collapse state for a tree (Int 0/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02353}02353 \textcolor{comment}{// This is optimized for efficient lookup (dichotomy into a contiguous buffer) and rare insertion (typically tied to user interactions aka max once a frame)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02354}02354 \textcolor{comment}{// You can use it as custom user storage for temporary values. Declare your own storage if, for example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02355}02355 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to manipulate the open/close state of a particular sub-\/tree in your interface (tree node uses Int 0/1 to store their state).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02356}02356 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to store custom debug data easily without adding or editing structures in your code (probably not efficient, but convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02357}02357 \textcolor{comment}{// Types are NOT stored, so it is up to you to make sure your Key don't collide with different types.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02400}02400 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02401}02401 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Manually clip large list of items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02402}02402 \textcolor{comment}{// If you have lots evenly spaced items and you have a random access to the list, you can perform coarse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02403}02403 \textcolor{comment}{// clipping based on visibility to only submit items that are in view.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02404}02404 \textcolor{comment}{// The clipper calculates the range of visible items and advance the cursor to compensate for the non-\/visible items we have skipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02405}02405 \textcolor{comment}{// (Dear ImGui already clip items based on their bounds but: it needs to first layout the item to do so, and generally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02406}02406 \textcolor{comment}{//  fetching/submitting your own data incurs additional cost. Coarse clipping using ImGuiListClipper allows you to easily}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02407}02407 \textcolor{comment}{//  scale using lists with tens of thousands of items without a problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02408}02408 \textcolor{comment}{// Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02409}02409 \textcolor{comment}{//   ImGuiListClipper clipper;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02410}02410 \textcolor{comment}{//   clipper.Begin(1000);         // We have 1000 elements, evenly spaced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02411}02411 \textcolor{comment}{//   while (clipper.Step())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02412}02412 \textcolor{comment}{//       for (int i = clipper.DisplayStart; i < clipper.DisplayEnd; i++)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02413}02413 \textcolor{comment}{//           ImGui::Text("{}line number \%d"{}, i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02414}02414 \textcolor{comment}{// Generally what happens is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02415}02415 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper lets you process the first element (DisplayStart = 0, DisplayEnd = 1) regardless of it being visible or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02416}02416 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit that one element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02417}02417 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper can measure the height of the first element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02418}02418 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper calculate the actual range of elements to display based on the current clipping rectangle, position the cursor before the first visible element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02419}02419 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit visible elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02420}02420 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The clipper also handles various subtleties related to keyboard/gamepad navigation, wrapping etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02421}\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{02421}} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02422}02422 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02423}02423     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             DisplayStart;       \textcolor{comment}{// First item to display, updated by each call to Step()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02424}02424     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             DisplayEnd;         \textcolor{comment}{// End of items to display (exclusive)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02465}02465 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: ImColor() implicitly converts colors to either ImU32 (packed 4x1 byte) or ImVec4 (4x1 float)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02496}02496 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawCallback: Draw callbacks for advanced uses [configurable type: override in imconfig.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02497}02497 \textcolor{comment}{// NB: You most likely do NOT need to use draw callbacks just to create your own widget or customized UI rendering,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02498}02498 \textcolor{comment}{// you can poke into the draw list for that! Draw callback may be useful for example to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02499}02499 \textcolor{comment}{//  A) Change your GPU render state,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02500}02500 \textcolor{comment}{//  B) render a complex 3D scene inside a UI element without an intermediate texture/render target, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02501}02501 \textcolor{comment}{// The expected behavior from your rendering function is 'if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL) \{ cmd.UserCallback(parent\_list, cmd); \} else \{ RenderTriangles() \}'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02502}02502 \textcolor{comment}{// If you want to override the signature of ImDrawCallback, you can simply use e.g. '\#define ImDrawCallback MyDrawCallback' (in imconfig.h) + update rendering backend accordingly.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02508}02508 \textcolor{comment}{// The renderer backend needs to handle this special value, otherwise it will crash trying to call a function at this address.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02509}02509 \textcolor{comment}{// This is useful for example if you submitted callbacks which you know have altered the render state and you want it to be restored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02510}02510 \textcolor{comment}{// It is not done by default because they are many perfectly useful way of altering render state for imgui contents (e.g. changing shader/blending settings before an Image call).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02584}02584 \textcolor{comment}{// (Legacy: bit 0 must always correspond to ImDrawFlags\_Closed to be backward compatible with old API using a bool. Bits 1..3 must be unused)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02585}02585 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImDrawFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02586}02586 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02587}02587     ImDrawFlags\_None                        = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02588}02588     ImDrawFlags\_Closed                      = 1 << 0, \textcolor{comment}{// PathStroke(), AddPolyline(): specify that shape should be closed (Important: this is always == 1 for legacy reason)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02589}02589     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft         = 1 << 4, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x01.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02590}02590     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight        = 1 << 5, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x02.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02591}02591     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft      = 1 << 6, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x04.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02592}02592     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight     = 1 << 7, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Wax 0x08.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02593}02593     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone            = 1 << 8, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): disable rounding on all corners (when rounding > 0.0f). This is NOT zero, NOT an implicit flag!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02594}02594     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTop             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02595}02595     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottom          = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02596}02596     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersLeft            = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02597}02597     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersRight           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02598}02598     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02599}02599     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersDefault\_        = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll, \textcolor{comment}{// Default to ALL corners if none of the \_RoundCornersXX flags are specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02600}02600     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersMask\_           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02603}02603 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImDrawList instance. Those are set automatically by ImGui:: functions from ImGuiIO settings, and generally not manipulated directly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02604}02604 \textcolor{comment}{// It is however possible to temporarily alter flags between calls to ImDrawList:: functions.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02606}02606 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02609}02609     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex  = 1 << 1,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased lines/borders using textures when possible. Require backend to render with bilinear filtering.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02614}02614 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw command list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02615}02615 \textcolor{comment}{// This is the low-\/level list of polygons that ImGui:: functions are filling. At the end of the frame,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02616}02616 \textcolor{comment}{// all command lists are passed to your ImGuiIO::RenderDrawListFn function for rendering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02617}02617 \textcolor{comment}{// Each dear imgui window contains its own ImDrawList. You can use ImGui::GetWindowDrawList() to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02618}02618 \textcolor{comment}{// access the current window draw list and draw custom primitives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02619}02619 \textcolor{comment}{// You can interleave normal ImGui:: calls and adding primitives to the current draw list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02620}02620 \textcolor{comment}{// In single viewport mode, top-\/left is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos (generally 0,0), bottom-\/right is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos+Size (generally io.DisplaySize).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02621}02621 \textcolor{comment}{// You are totally free to apply whatever transformation matrix to want to the data (depending on the use of the transformation you may want to apply it to ClipRect as well!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02622}02622 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: Primitives are always added to the list and not culled (culling is done at higher-\/level by ImGui:: functions), if you use this API a lot consider coarse culling your drawn objects.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02848}02848 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02849}02849 \textcolor{comment}{// Load and rasterize multiple TTF/OTF fonts into a same texture. The font atlas will build a single texture holding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02850}02850 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ One or more fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02851}02851 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Custom graphics data needed to render the shapes needed by Dear ImGui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02852}02852 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Mouse cursor shapes for software cursor rendering (unless setting 'Flags |= ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors' in the font atlas).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02853}02853 \textcolor{comment}{// It is the user-\/code responsibility to setup/build the atlas, then upload the pixel data into a texture accessible by your graphics api.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02854}02854 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Optionally, call any of the AddFont*** functions. If you don't call any, the default font embedded in the code will be loaded for you.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02855}02855 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call GetTexDataAsAlpha8() or GetTexDataAsRGBA32() to build and retrieve pixels data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02856}02856 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Upload the pixels data into a texture within your graphics system (see imgui\_impl\_xxxx.cpp examples)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02857}02857 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call SetTexID(my\_tex\_id); and pass the pointer/identifier to your texture in a format natural to your graphics API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02858}02858 \textcolor{comment}{//    This value will be passed back to you during rendering to identify the texture. Read FAQ entry about ImTextureID for more details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02859}02859 \textcolor{comment}{// Common pitfalls:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02860}02860 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you pass a 'glyph\_ranges' array to AddFont*** functions, you need to make sure that your array persist up until the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02861}02861 \textcolor{comment}{//   atlas is build (when calling GetTexData*** or Build()). We only copy the pointer, not the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02862}02862 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: By default, AddFontFromMemoryTTF() takes ownership of the data. Even though we are not writing to it, we will free the pointer on destruction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02863}02863 \textcolor{comment}{//   You can set font\_cfg-\/>FontDataOwnedByAtlas=false to keep ownership of your data and it won't be freed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02864}02864 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Even though many functions are suffixed with "{}TTF"{}, OTF data is supported just as well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l02865}02865 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is an old API and it is currently awkward for those and and various other reasons! We will address them in the future!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03029}03029     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoDecoration             = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Disable platform decorations: title bar, borders, etc. (generally set all windows, but if ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsDecoration is set we only set this on popups/tooltips)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03030}03030     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoTaskBarIcon            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Disable platform task bar icon (generally set on popups/tooltips, or all windows if ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsNoTaskBarIcon is set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03031}03031     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoFocusOnAppearing       = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Don't take focus when created.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03032}03032     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoFocusOnClick           = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Don't take focus when clicked on.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03033}03033     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoInputs                 = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Make mouse pass through so we can drag this window while peaking behind it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03034}03034     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoRendererClear          = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Renderer doesn't need to clear the framebuffer ahead (because we will fill it entirely).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03035}03035     ImGuiViewportFlags\_TopMost                  = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Display on top (for tooltips only).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03036}03036     ImGuiViewportFlags\_Minimized                = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Window is minimized, can skip render. When minimized we tend to avoid using the viewport pos/size for clipping window or testing if they are contained in the viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03037}03037     ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoAutoMerge              = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Avoid merging this window into another host window. This can only be set via ImGuiWindowClass viewport flags override (because we need to now ahead if we are going to create a viewport in the first place!).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03038}03038     ImGuiViewportFlags\_CanHostOtherWindows      = 1 << 12   \textcolor{comment}{// Main viewport: can host multiple imgui windows (secondary viewports are associated to a single window).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03039}03039 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03040}03040 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03041}03041 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Currently represents the Platform Window created by the application which is hosting our Dear ImGui windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03042}03042 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ With multi-\/viewport enabled, we extend this concept to have multiple active viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03043}03043 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In the future we will extend this concept further to also represent Platform Monitor and support a "{}no main platform window"{} operation mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03044}03044 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ About Main Area vs Work Area:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03045}03045 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Main Area = entire viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03046}03046 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Work Area = entire viewport minus sections used by main menu bars (for platform windows), or by task bar (for platform monitor).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03047}03047 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Windows are generally trying to stay within the Work Area of their host viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03048}\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{03048}} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03049}03049 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03050}03050     ImGuiID             ID;                     \textcolor{comment}{// Unique identifier for the viewport}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03051}03051     ImGuiViewportFlags  Flags;                  \textcolor{comment}{// See ImGuiViewportFlags\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03052}03052     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              Pos;                    \textcolor{comment}{// Main Area: Position of the viewport (Dear ImGui coordinates are the same as OS desktop/native coordinates)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03053}03053     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              Size;                   \textcolor{comment}{// Main Area: Size of the viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03054}03054     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              WorkPos;                \textcolor{comment}{// Work Area: Position of the viewport minus task bars, menus bars, status bars (>= Pos)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03055}03055     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              WorkSize;               \textcolor{comment}{// Work Area: Size of the viewport minus task bars, menu bars, status bars (<= Size)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03056}03056     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}               DpiScale;               \textcolor{comment}{// 1.0f = 96 DPI = No extra scale.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03057}03057     ImGuiID             ParentViewportId;       \textcolor{comment}{// (Advanced) 0: no parent. Instruct the platform backend to setup a parent/child relationship between platform windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03058}03058     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_data}{ImDrawData}}*         DrawData;               \textcolor{comment}{// The ImDrawData corresponding to this viewport. Valid after Render() and until the next call to NewFrame().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03059}03059 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03060}03060     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform/Backend Dependent Data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03061}03061     \textcolor{comment}{// Our design separate the Renderer and Platform backends to facilitate combining default backends with each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03062}03062     \textcolor{comment}{// When our create your own backend for a custom engine, it is possible that both Renderer and Platform will be handled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03063}03063     \textcolor{comment}{// by the same system and you may not need to use all the UserData/Handle fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03064}03064     \textcolor{comment}{// The library never uses those fields, they are merely storage to facilitate backend implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03065}03065     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               RendererUserData;       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the renderer (e.g. swap chain, framebuffers etc.). generally set by your Renderer\_CreateWindow function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03066}03066     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformUserData;       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the OS / platform (e.g. windowing info, render context). generally set by your Platform\_CreateWindow function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03067}03067     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformHandle;         \textcolor{comment}{// void* for FindViewportByPlatformHandle(). (e.g. suggested to use natural platform handle such as HWND, GLFWWindow*, SDL\_Window*)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03068}03068     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               PlatformHandleRaw;      \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold lower-\/level, platform-\/native window handle (under Win32 this is expected to be a HWND, unused for other platforms), when using an abstraction layer like GLFW or SDL (where PlatformHandle would be a SDL\_Window*)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03069}03069     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestMove;    \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested move (e.g. window was moved by the OS / host window manager, authoritative position will be OS window position)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03070}03070     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestResize;  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested resize (e.g. window was resized by the OS / host window manager, authoritative size will be OS window size)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03071}03071     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                PlatformRequestClose;   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform window requested closure (e.g. window was moved by the OS / host window manager, e.g. pressing ALT-\/F4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03072}03072 }
