\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03080}03080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03081}03081 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03082}03082 \textcolor{comment}{// [SECTION] Platform Dependent Interfaces (for e.g. multi-\/viewport support)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03083}03083 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03084}03084 \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] (Optional) This is completely optional, for advanced users!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03085}03085 \textcolor{comment}{// If you are new to Dear ImGui and trying to integrate it into your engine, you can probably ignore this for now.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03086}03086 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03087}03087 \textcolor{comment}{// This feature allows you to seamlessly drag Dear ImGui windows outside of your application viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03088}03088 \textcolor{comment}{// This is achieved by creating new Platform/OS windows on the fly, and rendering into them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03089}03089 \textcolor{comment}{// Dear ImGui manages the viewport structures, and the backend create and maintain one Platform/OS window for each of those viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03090}03090 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03091}03091 \textcolor{comment}{// See Glossary https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/wiki/Glossary for details about some of the terminology.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03092}03092 \textcolor{comment}{// See Thread https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/1542 for gifs, news and questions about this evolving feature.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03093}03093 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03094}03094 \textcolor{comment}{// About the coordinates system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03095}03095 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When multi-\/viewports are enabled, all Dear ImGui coordinates become absolute coordinates (same as OS coordinates!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03096}03096 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ So e.g. ImGui::SetNextWindowPos(ImVec2(0,0)) will position a window relative to your primary monitor!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03097}03097 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you want to position windows relative to your main application viewport, use ImGui::GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos as a base position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03098}03098 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03099}03099 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a default backend from the examples/ folder:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03100}03100 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03101}03101 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      The backend initialization will setup all necessary ImGuiPlatformIO's functions and update monitors info every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03102}03102 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03103}03103 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03104}03104 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03105}03105 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a custom backend:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03106}03106 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important:    THIS IS NOT EASY TO DO and comes with many subtleties not described here!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03107}03107 \textcolor{comment}{//                 It's also an experimental feature, so some of the requirements may evolve.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03108}03108 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Consider using default backends if you can. Either way, carefully follow and refer to examples/ backends for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03109}03109 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03110}03110 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      Hook ImGuiPlatformIO's Platform\_* and Renderer\_* callbacks (see below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03111}03111 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Set 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports' and 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03112}03112 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update ImGuiPlatformIO's Monitors list every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03113}03113 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update MousePos every frame, in absolute coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03114}03114 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03115}03115 \textcolor{comment}{//                 You may skip calling RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() if its API is not convenient for your needs. Read comments below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03116}03116 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03117}03117 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03118}03118 \textcolor{comment}{// About ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03119}03119 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This function is a mostly a \_helper\_ for the common-\/most cases, and to facilitate using default backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03120}03120 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can check its simple source code to understand what it does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03121}03121 \textcolor{comment}{//   It basically iterates secondary viewports and call 4 functions that are setup in ImGuiPlatformIO, if available:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03122}03122 \textcolor{comment}{//     Platform\_RenderWindow(), Renderer\_RenderWindow(), Platform\_SwapBuffers(), Renderer\_SwapBuffers()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03123}03123 \textcolor{comment}{//   Those functions pointers exists only for the benefit of RenderPlatformWindowsDefault().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03124}03124 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you have very specific rendering needs (e.g. flipping multiple swap-\/chain simultaneously, unusual sync/threading issues, etc.),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03125}03125 \textcolor{comment}{//   you may be tempted to ignore RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() and write customized code to perform your renderingg.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03126}03126 \textcolor{comment}{//   You may decide to setup the platform\_io's *RenderWindow and *SwapBuffers pointers and call your functions through those pointers,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03127}03127 \textcolor{comment}{//   or you may decide to never setup those pointers and call your code directly. They are a convenience, not an obligatory interface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03128}03128 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03129}03129 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03130}03130 \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Access via ImGui::GetPlatformIO()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03131}\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_platform_i_o}{03131}} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_platform_i_o}{ImGuiPlatformIO}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03132}03132 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03133}03133     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03134}03134     \textcolor{comment}{// Input -\/ Backend interface/functions + Monitor List}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03135}03135     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03136}03136 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03137}03137     \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Platform functions (e.g. Win32, GLFW, SDL2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03138}03138     \textcolor{comment}{// For reference, the second column shows which function are generally calling the Platform Functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03139}03139     \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ImGui::NewFrame()                        \string~ beginning of the dear imgui frame: read info from platform/OS windows (latest size/position)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03140}03140     \textcolor{comment}{//   F = ImGui::Begin(), ImGui::EndFrame()        \string~ during the dear imgui frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03141}03141     \textcolor{comment}{//   U = ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows()           \string~ after the dear imgui frame: create and update all platform/OS windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03142}03142     \textcolor{comment}{//   R = ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault()    \string~ render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03143}03143     \textcolor{comment}{//   D = ImGui::DestroyPlatformWindows()          \string~ shutdown}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03144}03144     \textcolor{comment}{// The general idea is that NewFrame() we will read the current Platform/OS state, and UpdatePlatformWindows() will write to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03145}03145     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03146}03146     \textcolor{comment}{// The functions are designed so we can mix and match 2 imgui\_impl\_xxxx files, one for the Platform (\string~window/input handling), one for Renderer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03147}03147     \textcolor{comment}{// Custom engine backends will often provide both Platform and Renderer interfaces and so may not need to use all functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03148}03148     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform functions are typically called before their Renderer counterpart, apart from Destroy which are called the other way.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03149}03149 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03150}03150     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform function -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ Called by -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03160}03160     bool    (*Platform\_GetWindowMinimized)(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}* vp);              \textcolor{comment}{// N . . . .  // Get platform window minimized state. When minimized, we generally won't attempt to get/set size and contents will be culled more easily}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l03161}03161     void    (*Platform\_SetWindowTitle)(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}* vp, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str); \textcolor{comment}{// . .
